<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><b>дви́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>гать</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:двинуть.html>дви́нуть</a>.

<p><b>дви́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:га.html>га</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ться</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:двинуться.html>дви́нуться</a>.

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-двиг-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движение</a> (431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvižénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:движение.html>движе́ний</a></b>)

<p><b>дви<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-движ-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ениj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:двинуться.html>дви́нуться</a> (1714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двинуть.html>дви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двинуться.html>дви́нуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvínutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двигаться.html>дви́гаться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to move</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go crazy, to lose one's wits</li></ol>

<p><b>дви́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нуть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***двое.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a> (660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvóje</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>two (in a group together), two of them
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvóje</b> detéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>two</b> children</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvóje</b> časóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>two</b> watches</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvóje</b> očkóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>two</b> pairs of glasses</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvóje</b> iz nas</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>two</b> of us</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nas býlo <b>dvóje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there were <b>two</b> of us</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The nominative of a collective numeral governs the genitive plural of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. For the other cases the noun, pronoun, or adjective will be in the same case (except when meaning "a pair of"). Not used with feminine nouns. Used mostly when speaking of children and with a few nouns that are used in the plural only, such as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">časý</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očkí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or with pronouns.</li></ul>
<p>Examples:
</p>
<ul><li>In the nominative, governing a genitive plural:
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:навстречу.html>навстре́чу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>шли́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парень.html>парне́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Navstréču mne šli <b>dvóje</b> parnéj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Two</b> guys came to meet me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найтись.html>найдётся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ножницы.html>но́жниц</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá najdjótsja <b>dvóje</b> nóžnic.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have <b>two</b> (pairs of) scissors.</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">With me are <b>two</b> (pairs of) scissors.</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>In the accusative, governing a genitive plural when meaning "a pair of":
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>взять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>собо́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:носок.html>носко́в</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nádo vzjatʹ s sobój <b>dvóje</b> noskóv.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">You need to take <b>a pair of</b> socks with you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>In the accusative, governing an accusative plural when meaning "two":
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:там.html>там</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встретить.html>встре́тил</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>двои́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сослуживец.html>сослужи́вцев</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja tam vstrétil <b>dvoíx</b> soslužívcev.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I met <b>two</b> of my colleagues there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>

***двоечник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:двоечник.html>дво́ечник</a> (24993)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvójka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The USSR and now the Russian Federation and other Ex-Soviet republics used/use a five-point academic grading system where <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">two, number 2</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> denotes hardly any knowledge, below average, the first level of failing.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоечник.html>дво́ечник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvóješnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоечник.html>дво́ечника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоечник.html>дво́ечники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоечник.html>дво́ечников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">дво́ечница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pupil with only the lowest mark "two" in his record.</li>
<li>(by extension) anyone who is a bad performer</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dvójka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>дво́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>еч<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́к</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дв-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-оj-еч-ник</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>уча́щийся</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:получающий.html>получа́ющий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плохой.html>плохи́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оценка.html>оце́нки</a>, неуспевающий <a href = vnd.unilang:ученик.html>учени́к</a>.</li>

</ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йка</a> (9280)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двое.html>дво́е</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvóje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>two</li>
<li><i>(mark)</i> two <i>(out of five)</i>, poor; D mark, D grade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ставить.html>ста́влю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йку</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Stávlju tebé za éto <b>dvójku</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I grade your work as very poor.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:получить.html>получи́л</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йку</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:история.html>исто́рии</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On polučíl <b>dvójku</b> po istórii.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He got a poor grade for history; he didn't pass the history exam.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>dvójku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">awfully, wretchedly, couldn't be worse</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> two, deuce
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:козырной.html>козы́рная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kozýrnaja <b>dvójka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">two of trumps</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двойка.html>дво́йка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:червь.html>черве́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvójka</b> červéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the two of hearts</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>No 2 (bus, tram, etc.)</li>
<li>pair-oar boat, pair, double sculls</li>
<li>two-piece suit</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двойственный.html>дво́йственный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvójstvennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dual
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двойственный.html>дво́йственное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>число́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvójstvennoje čisló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dual number</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>two-faced, double-faced

<li>bipartite
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:двойственный.html>дво́йственное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:соглашение.html>соглаше́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvójstvennoje</b> soglašénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>bipartite</b> agreement</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dvòrъ</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двора́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>дворы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>дворо́в</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дворовый.html>дворо́вый</a> (14705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двор.html>двор</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дворовый.html>дворо́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvoróvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> court, yard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дворовый.html>дворо́вые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́ди</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvoróvyje</b> ljúdi</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>court</b> staff <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a prince's court</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дворовый.html>дворо́вая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvoróvaja</b> sobáka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">1) watchdog; 2) mongrel</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>yard</b> dog</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дворовый.html>дворо́вые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:постройка.html>постро́йки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dvoróvyje</b> postrójki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">outbuildings; outhouses</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>yard</b> buildings</span>”)</div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дворянство.html>дворя́нство</a> (14191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дворянство.html>дворя́нство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvorjánstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дворянство.html>дворя́нства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дворянство.html>дворя́нства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дворянство.html>дворя́нств</a></b>)

***двоюродный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a> (7259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дъвою родꙋ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dŭvoju rodu</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of two generations</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дъвою</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dŭvoju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is a genitive dual form, from which <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ю-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ju-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> was extracted and used analogously in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:троюродный.html>трою́родный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trojúrodnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">четверою́родный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">četverojúrodnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dvojúrodnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">denotes a relative in the same generation as the head noun but one degree greater in separation</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дед.html>дед</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvojúrodnyj ded</i> ― <span class="e-translation">great uncle, grandfather’s generation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дядя.html>дя́дя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvojúrodnyj djádja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">male first cousin once removed, uncle’s generation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>брат</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvojúrodnyj brat</i> ― <span class="e-translation">male first cousin, brother’s generation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:племянник.html>племя́нник</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvojúrodnyj plemjánnik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">male first cousin once removed, nephew’s generation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внук.html>внук</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvojúrodnyj vnuk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">grandnephew, grandson’s generation</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правнук.html>пра́внук</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dvojúrodnyj právnuk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">great-grandnephew, great-grandson’s generation</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>There is no single equivalent of this term in English. It is applied to close relations (e.g. brothers, uncles, grandfathers) and indicates a relation that is in the same generation as the term being modified, but is one degree greater in separation in terms of the closest common ancestor. For example, the <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a></span> equivalent of one's brother is one's first cousin, because one has a common father with one's brother, but a common grandfather with one's first cousin. Similarly, the <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a></span> equivalent of one's grandfather is one's great uncle, because the nearest common ancestor between one and one's grandfather is the grandfather himself, whereas the nearest common ancestor between one and one's great uncle is one's great-grandfather. (The <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двоюродный.html>двою́родный</a></span> equivalent of one's father is one's uncle, but there is already a special term for this relationship.)</li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>дво<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ю́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-дв-</b>; суффикс: <b>-оj</b>; интерфикс: <b>-ю-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-род-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:двуколка.html>двуко́лка</a> (31664)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>дву<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кол.html>ко́л</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

***де.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a> (2559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дѣеть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">děetĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to say</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle_2">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">de</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> says <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used informally to mark reported speech</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">она́-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ла</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná-<b>de</b> ne znála.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She says she didn’t know.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Я-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:виноватый.html>винова́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja-<b>de</b> sam vinovát</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I say it's my own fault.</span></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1876</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9C%D0%B5%D1%89%D0%B5%D1%80%D1%81%D0%BA%D0%B8%D0%B9,_%D0%92%D0%BB%D0%B0%D0%B4%D0%B8%D0%BC%D0%B8%D1%80_%D0%9F%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="w:ru:Мещерский, Владимир Петрович"><a href = vnd.unilang:князь.html>князь</a> Владимир Петрович Мещерский</a>,  “Русскому дворянству”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>Ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:консерватор.html>консерва́тора</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> смущаетъ <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a> дворяни́нъ-помѣщикъ мыслiю, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> онъ оди́нъ себѣ скажетъ <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> здравыя <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a> – <a href = vnd.unilang:толк.html>толку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> будетъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> что-<b><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> многимъ <a href = vnd.unilang:собраться.html>собра́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́ти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:высказать.html>вы́сказать</a> общимъ собранiемъ.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">I da ne smuščajet sebjá dvorjanín-poměščik mysliju, što jésli on odín sebě skažet vse éti zdravyja mýsli – tolku ne budet, a što-<b>de</b> nado nado mnogim sobrátʹsja i éti mýsli výskazatʹ obščim sobranijem.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The noble landlord shouldn't confuse himself by the thought that would he tell all those sensible thoughts by himself it won't make any sense but many should gather and tell all those thoughts by full gathering.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">govorít</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говоря́т</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">govorját</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дескать.html>де́скать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">déskatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мол.html>мол</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mol</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">débile</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">debilis</i>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>деби́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">debíl</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дебил.html>деби́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дебил.html>деби́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дебил.html>деби́лов</a></b>)
</p>

***дебри.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дебри.html>де́бри</a> (15139)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дъбрь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dŭbrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> : <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">дьбрь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dĭbrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dьbrь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">valley, ravine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*dubr-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰubr-</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dʰewbʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deep</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дебри.html>де́бри</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">débri</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дебри.html>де́брей</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>thickets, jungle, wilderness, wilds, bush</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> maze, labyrinth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запутаться.html>запу́таться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дебри.html>де́брях</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zapútatʹsja v <b>débrjax</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be lost in the maze (of something), to get bogged down (in a difficult problem)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
